[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind[0m  [-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [expresâ€[m
       sion][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[0m.  GNU [1mfind[0m searches  the[m
       directory  tree rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating the given[m
       expression from left to right, according to the rules  of  precedence  (see[m
       section OPERATORS), until the outcome is known (the left hand side is false[m
       for [4mand[24m operations, true for [4mor[24m), at which point [1mfind[0m moves on to the  next[m
       file name.  If no starting-point is specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If  you  are  using [1mfind[0m in an environment where security is important (for[m
       example if you are using it to search  directories  that  are  writable  by[m
       other  users), you should read the `Security Considerations' chapter of the[m
       findutils documentation, which is called [1mFinding[0m [1mFiles[0m and comes with findâ€[m
       utils.   That  document also includes a lot more detail and discussion than[m
       this manual page, so you may find it a more useful source of information.[m
[m
[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       The [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m options control the treatment of  symbolic  links.   Comâ€[m
       mand-line  arguments  following these are taken to be names of files or diâ€[m
       rectories to be examined, up to the first argument that begins with `-', or[m
       the  argument  `('  or  `!'.  That argument and any following arguments are[m
       taken to be the expression describing what is to be searched  for.   If  no[m
       paths are given, the current directory is used.  If no expression is given,[m
       the expression [1m-print[0m is used  (but  you  should  probably  consider  using[m
       [1m-print0[0m instead, anyway).[m
[m
       This  manual  page talks about `options' within the expression list.  These[m
       options control the behaviour of [1mfind[0m but are specified  immediately  after[m
       the last path name.  The five `real' options [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m, [1m-P[0m, [1m-D[0m and [1m-O[0m must apâ€[m
       pear before the first path name, if at all.  A double dash [1m--[0m  could  theoâ€[m
       retically  be  used to signal that any remaining arguments are not options,[m
       but this does not really work due to the way [1mfind[0m determines the end of the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       following path arguments: it does that by reading until an expression arguâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       ment comes (which also starts with a `-').  Now, if a path  argument  would[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       start  with a `-', then [1mfind[0m would treat it as expression argument instead.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       Thus, to ensure that all start points are taken as such, and especially  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       prevent  that  wildcard patterns expanded by the calling shell are not misâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       takenly treated as expression arguments, it is generally  safer  to  prefix[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       wildcards  or  dubious  path names with either `./' or to use absolute path[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       names starting with '/'.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       -P     Never follow symbolic links.  This is the default  behaviour.   When[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              [1mfind[0m  examines  or prints information about files, and the file is a[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              symbolic link, the information used shall be taken from the  properâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              ties of the symbolic link itself.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       -L     Follow  symbolic  links.   When  [1mfind[0m examines or prints information[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              about files, the information used shall be taken from the properties[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              of  the file to which the link points, not from the link itself (unâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              less it is a broken symbolic link or [1mfind[0m is unable to  examine  the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              file to which the link points).  Use of this option implies [1m-noleaf[0m.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              If you later use the [1m-P[0m option, [1m-noleaf[0m will still be in effect.  If[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              [1m-L[0m is in effect and [1mfind[0m discovers a symbolic link to a subdirectory[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              during its search, the subdirectory pointed to by the symbolic  link[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              will be searched.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 25 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              When  the  [1m-L[0m  option  is in effect, the [1m-type[0m predicate will always[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 26 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              match against the type of the file that a symbolic  link  points  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              rather  than  the  link itself (unless the symbolic link is broken).[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 28 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              Actions that can cause symbolic links to become broken while [1mfind[0m is[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 29 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              executing  (for  example  [1m-delete[0m) can give rise to confusing behavâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 30 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              iour.  Using [1m-L[0m causes the [1m-lname[0m and [1m-ilname[0m predicates  always  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 31 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              return false.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 32 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 33 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       -H     Do  not  follow  symbolic links, except while processing the command[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 34 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              line arguments.  When [1mfind[0m  examines  or  prints  information  about[m

[m
       -Olevel[m
              Enables query optimisation.  The  [1mfind[0m  program  reorders  tests  to[m
              speed  up  execution  while  preserving the overall effect; that is,[m
              predicates with side effects are  not  reordered  relative  to  each[m
              other.   The  optimisations performed at each optimisation level are[m
              as follows.[m
[m
              0      Equivalent to optimisation level 1.[m
[m
              1      This is the default optimisation level and corresponds to the[m
                     traditional  behaviour.   Expressions  are  reordered so that[m
                     tests based only on the names of files (for example [1m-name[0m and[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 115 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K                     [1m-regex[0m) are performed first.[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 117 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              2      Any [1m-type[0m or [1m-xtype[0m tests are performed after any tests based[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 118 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K                     only on the names of files, but before any tests that require[m
                     information from the inode.  On many modern versions of Unix,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 120 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[Kjj[K[7m Manual page find(1) line 120 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KESCESC[K[7m Manual page find(1) line 120 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     file types are returned by [1mreaddir()[0m and so these  predicates[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 121 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     are faster to evaluate than predicates which need to stat the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 122 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     file first.  If you use the [1m-fstype[0m [4mFOO[24m predicate and specify[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 123 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     a filesystem type [4mFOO[24m which is not known (that is, present in[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 124 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     `/etc/mtab') at the  time  [1mfind[0m  starts,  that  predicate  is[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 125 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     equivalent to [1m-false[0m.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 126 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 127 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              3      At  this  optimisation level, the full cost-based query optiâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 128 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     miser is enabled.  The order of tests  is  modified  so  that[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 129 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     cheap  (i.e.  fast) tests are performed first and more expenâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 130 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     sive ones are performed later,  if  necessary.   Within  each[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 131 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     cost  band, predicates are evaluated earlier or later accordâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 132 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     ing to whether they are likely to succeed or  not.   For  [1m-o[0m,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 133 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     predicates which are likely to succeed are evaluated earlier,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 134 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     and for [1m-a[0m, predicates which are likely to fail are evaluated[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 135 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                     earlier.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 136 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 137 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              The  cost-based  optimiser  has a fixed idea of how likely any given[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 138 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              test is to succeed.  In some cases the probability takes account  of[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 139 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              the  specific nature of the test (for example, [1m-type[0m [1mf[0m is assumed to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 140 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              be more likely to succeed than [1m-type[0m [1mc[0m).  The  cost-based  optimiser[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 141 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              is  currently  being evaluated.  If it does not actually improve the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 142 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              performance of [1mfind[0m, it will be removed again.  Conversely,  optimiâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 143 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              sations  that  prove to be reliable, robust and effective may be enâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 144 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              abled at lower optimisation levels over time.  However, the  default[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 145 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              behaviour  (i.e.  optimisation  level  1) will not be changed in the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 146 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              4.3.x release series.  The findutils test suite runs all  the  tests[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 147 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              on  [1mfind[0m  at  each optimisation level and ensures that the result is[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 148 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K              the same.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 149 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[m

[10;1H              dard output) and return either  true  or  false,  usually  based  on[m
[11;1H              whether  or  not they are successful.  The [1m-print[0m action for example[m
[12;1H              prints the name of the current file on the standard output.[m
[13;1H[m
[14;1H       Global options[m
[15;1H              Global options affect the operation of tests and  actions  specified[m
[16;1H              on any part of the command line.  Global options always return true.[m
[17;1H              The [1m-depth[0m option for example makes [1mfind[0m traverse the file system in[m
[18;1H              a depth-first order.[m
[19;1H[m
[20;1H       Positional options[m
[21;1H              Positional  options  affect only tests or actions which follow them.[m
[22;1H              Positional options always return true.  The  [1m-regextype[0m  option  for[m
[23;1H              example is positional, specifying the regular expression dialect for[m
[24;1H              regular expressions occurring later on the command line.[m
[25;1H[m
[26;1H       Operators[m
[27;1H              Operators join together the other items within the expression.  They[m
[28;1H              include  for example [1m-o[0m (meaning logical OR) and [1m-a[0m (meaning logical[m
[29;1H              AND).  Where an operator is missing, [1m-a[0m is assumed.[m
[30;1H[m
[31;1H       The [1m-print[0m action is performed on all files for which the whole  expression[m
[32;1H       is  true, unless it contains an action other than [1m-prune[0m or [1m-quit[0m.  Actions[m
[33;1H       which inhibit the default [1m-print[0m are [1m-delete[0m, [1m-exec[0m, [1m-execdir[0m, [1m-ok[0m, [1m-okdir[0m,[m
[34;1H       [1m-fls[0m, [1m-fprint[0m, [1m-fprintf[0m, [1m-ls[0m, [1m-print[0m and [1m-printf[0m.[m
[35;1H[m
[36;1H       The [1m-delete[0m action also acts like an option (since it implies [1m-depth[0m).[m
[37;1H[m
[38;1H   [1mPOSITIONAL[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[39;1H       Positional  options  always  return true.  They affect only tests occurring[m
[40;1H       later on the command line.[m
[41;1H[1;1H       files and what we do with the files that were matched.   An  expression  is[m
[2;1H       composed of a sequence of things:[m
[3;1H[m
[4;1H       Tests  Tests  return  a  true  or false value, usually on the basis of some[m
[5;1H              property of a file we are considering.  The [1m-empty[0m test for  example[m
[6;1H              is true only when the current file is empty.[m

       -depth Process each [7mdirectory[27m's contents before the [7mdirectory[27m itself.   The[m
              -delete action also implies [1m-depth[0m.[m

       -help, --help[m
              Print a summary of the command-line usage of [1mfind[0m and exit.[m
[m
       -ignore_readdir_race[m
              Normally,  [1mfind[0m  will  emit an error message when it fails to stat a[m
              file.  If you give this option and a file  is  deleted  between  the[m
              time [1mfind[0m reads the name of the file from the [7mdirectory[27m and the time[m
              it tries to stat the file, no error message will  be  issued.   This[m
              also  applies  to  files or directories whose names are given on the[m
              command line.  This option takes effect at the time the command line[m
              is read, which means that you cannot search one part of the filesysâ€[m
              tem with this option on and part of it with this option off (if  you[m
              need  to  do that, you will need to issue two [1mfind[0m commands instead,[m
              one with the option and one without it).[m
[m
              Furthermore, [1mfind[0m with the [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m option  will  ignore[m
              errors  of  the  [1m-delete[0m action in the case the file has disappeared[m
              since the parent [7mdirectory[27m was read: it will not output an error diâ€[m
              agnostic, and the return code of the [1m-delete[0m action will be true.[m
[m
       -maxdepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Descend  at  most [4mlevels[24m (a non-negative integer) levels of directoâ€[m
              ries below the starting-points.  Using [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m means only  apply[m
              the tests and actions to the starting-points themselves.[m
[m
       -mindepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Do not apply any tests or actions at levels less than [4mlevels[24m (a non-[m
              negative integer).  Using [1m-mindepth[0m [1m1[0m means process all files except[m
              the starting-points.[m

              When  the  [1m-L[0m  option  is in effect, the [1m-type[0m predicate will always[m

              rather  than  the  link itself (unless the symbolic link is broken).[m
              Actions that can cause symbolic links to become broken while [1mfind[0m is[m
              executing  (for  example  [1m-delete[0m) can give rise to confusing behavâ€[m
              iour.  Using [1m-L[0m causes the [1m-lname[0m and [1m-ilname[0m predicates  always  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 31 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              return false.[m
[m
       -H     Do  not  follow  symbolic links, except while processing the command[m
              line arguments.  When [1mfind[0m  examines  or  prints  information  about[m
              files,  the  information  used shall be taken from the properties of[m
              the symbolic link itself.  The only exception to this  behaviour  is[m
              when  a  file  specified on the command line is a symbolic link, and[m
              the link can be resolved.  For that situation, the information  used[m
              is taken from whatever the link points to (that is, the link is folâ€[m
              lowed).  The information about the link itself is used as a fallback[m
              if  the file pointed to by the symbolic link cannot be examined.  If[m
              [1m-H[0m is in effect and one of the paths specified on the  command  line[m
              is  a  symbolic  link to a [7mdirectory[27m, the contents of that [7mdirectory[27m[m
              will be examined (though of course [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m would prevent this).[m
[m
       If more than one of [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m is specified, each overrides the  others;[m
       the  last  one appearing on the command line takes effect.  Since it is the[m
       default, the [1m-P[0m option should be considered to be in effect  unless  either[m
       [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m is specified.[m
[m
       GNU  [1mfind[0m  frequently stats files during the processing of the command line[m
       itself, before any searching has begun.   These  options  also  affect  how[m
       those  arguments  are processed.  Specifically, there are a number of tests[m
       that compare files listed on the command line against a file  we  are  curâ€[m
       rently  considering.   In each case, the file specified on the command line[m
       will have been examined and some of its properties will  have  been  saved.[m
       If  the  named file is in fact a symbolic link, and the [1m-P[0m option is in efâ€[m
       fect (or if neither [1m-H[0m nor [1m-L[0m were specified), the information used for the[m
       comparison  will be taken from the properties of the symbolic link.  Otherâ€[m
       wise, it will be taken from the properties of the file the link points  to.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 61 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       If  [1mfind[0m  cannot  follow  the link (for example because it has insufficient[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 62 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       privileges or the link points to a nonexistent file) the properties of  the[m
       link itself will be used.[m
[m
       When  the  [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m options are in effect, any symbolic links listed as the[m
       argument of [1m-newer[0m will be dereferenced, and the timestamp  will  be  taken[m
       from  the  file  to which the symbolic link points.  The same consideration[m
       applies to [1m-newerXY[0m, [1m-anewer[0m and [1m-cnewer[0m.[m
[m
       The [1m-follow[0m option has a similar effect to [1m-L[0m, though it  takes  effect  at[m
       the  point where it appears (that is, if [1m-L[0m is not used but [1m-follow[0m is, any[m
       symbolic links appearing after [1m-follow[0m on the command line will be dereferâ€[m
       enced, and those before it will not).[m

       -Olevel[m
              Enables query optimisation.  The  [1mfind[0m  program  reorders  tests  to[m
              speed  up  execution  while  preserving the overall effect; that is,[m
              predicates with side effects are  not  reordered  relative  to  each[m
              other.   The  optimisations performed at each optimisation level are[m
              as follows.[m
[m
              0      Equivalent to optimisation level 1.[m
[m
              1      This is the default optimisation level and corresponds to the[m
                     traditional  behaviour.   Expressions  are  reordered so that[m
                     tests based only on the names of files (for example [1m-name[0m and[m
                     [1m-regex[0m) are performed first.[m
[m
              2      Any [1m-type[0m or [1m-xtype[0m tests are performed after any tests based[m
                     only on the names of files, but before any tests that require[m
                     information from the inode.  On many modern versions of Unix,[m
                     file types are returned by [1mreaddir()[0m and so these  predicates[m
                     are faster to evaluate than predicates which need to stat the[m
                     file first.  If you use the [1m-fstype[0m [4mFOO[24m predicate and specify[m
                     a filesystem type [4mFOO[24m which is not known (that is, present in[m
                     `/etc/mtab') at the  time  [1mfind[0m  starts,  that  predicate  is[m
                     equivalent to [1m-false[0m.[m
[m
              3      At  this  optimisation level, the full cost-based query optiâ€[m
                     miser is enabled.  The order of tests  is  modified  so  that[m
                     cheap  (i.e.  fast) tests are performed first and more expenâ€[m
                     sive ones are performed later,  if  necessary.   Within  each[m
                     cost  band, predicates are evaluated earlier or later accordâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 132 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
       -depth Process each [7mdirectory[27m's contents before the [7mdirectory[27m itself.   The[m
              -delete action also implies [1m-depth[0m.[m

       -help, --help[m

       -ignore_readdir_race[m
              Normally,  [1mfind[0m  will  emit an error message when it fails to stat a[m
              file.  If you give this option and a file  is  deleted  between  the[m
              time [1mfind[0m reads the name of the file from the [7mdirectory[27m and the time[m
              it tries to stat the file, no error message will  be  issued.   This[m
              also  applies  to  files or directories whose names are given on the[m
              command line.  This option takes effect at the time the command line[m
              is read, which means that you cannot search one part of the filesysâ€[m
              tem with this option on and part of it with this option off (if  you[m
              need  to  do that, you will need to issue two [1mfind[0m commands instead,[m
              one with the option and one without it).[m
[m
              Furthermore, [1mfind[0m with the [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m option  will  ignore[m
              errors  of  the  [1m-delete[0m action in the case the file has disappeared[m
              since the parent [7mdirectory[27m was read: it will not output an error diâ€[m
              agnostic, and the return code of the [1m-delete[0m action will be true.[m
[m
       -maxdepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Descend  at  most [4mlevels[24m (a non-negative integer) levels of directoâ€[m
              ries below the starting-points.  Using [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m means only  apply[m
              the tests and actions to the starting-points themselves.[m
[m
       -mindepth [4mlevels[24m[m

              negative integer).  Using [1m-mindepth[0m [1m1[0m means process all files except[m

       -noignore_readdir_race[m

[m
       -noleaf[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 283 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              Do not optimize by assuming that directories contain 2 fewer  subdiâ€[m
              rectories  than  their  hard link count.  This option is needed when[m
              searching filesystems that do not  follow  the  Unix  [7mdirectory[27m-link[m
              convention, such as CD-ROM or MS-DOS filesystems or AFS volume mount[m
              points.  Each [7mdirectory[27m on a normal Unix filesystem has at  least  2[m

              tories (if any) each have a `..' entry  linked  to  that  [7mdirectory[27m.[m
              When  [1mfind[0m  is  examining  a [7mdirectory[27m, after it has statted 2 fewer[m
              subdirectories than the [7mdirectory[27m's link count, it  knows  that  the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 292 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              rest  of  the  entries  in the [7mdirectory[27m are non-directories (`leaf'[m
              files in the [7mdirectory[27m tree).  If only the files' names need  to  be[m
              examined,  there  is  no need to stat them; this gives a significant[m

[7m Manual page find(1) line 303 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       Some tests, for example [1m-newerXY[0m and [1m-samefile[0m,  allow  comparison  between[m

       [1mstat[0m(2) system call fails for it), an error message is issued, and [1mfind[0m exâ€[m

[m

       [4m+n[24m     for greater than [4mn[24m,[m
[m

[7m Manual page find(1) line 325 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              ago.[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 327 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       -anewer [4mreference[24m[m
              Time of the last access of the current file is more recent than that[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 329 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              of the last data modification of the [4mreference[24m file.   If  [4mreference[24m[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 330 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              is  a symbolic link and the [1m-H[0m option or the [1m-L[0m option is in effect,[m

[7m Manual page find(1) line 333 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
       -empty File is empty and is either a regular file or a [7mdirectory[27m.[m

       -executable[m
              Matches files which are executable and directories which are searchâ€[m
              able (in a file name resolution sense) by the  current  user.   This[m
              takes  into account access control lists and other permissions arteâ€[m
              facts which the [1m-perm[0m test ignores.  This test makes use of the  [1macâ€[0m[m
              [1mcess[0m(2)  system  call,  and so can be fooled by NFS servers which do[m

       -newerXY [4mreference[24m[m

[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind[0m  [-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [expresâ€[m
       sion][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[0m.  GNU [1mfind[0m searches  the[m
       directory  tree rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating the given[m
       expression from left to right, according to the rules  of  precedence  (see[m
       section OPERATORS), until the outcome is known (the left hand side is false[m
       for [4mand[24m operations, true for [4mor[24m), at which point [1mfind[0m moves on to the  next[m
       file name.  If no starting-point is specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If  you  are  using [1mfind[0m in an environment where security is important (for[m
       example if you are using it to search  directories  that  are  writable  by[m
       other  users), you should read the `Security Considerations' chapter of the[m
       findutils documentation, which is called [1mFinding[0m [1mFiles[0m and comes with findâ€[m
       utils.   That  document also includes a lot more detail and discussion than[m
       this manual page, so you may find it a more useful source of information.[m
[m
[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       The [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m options control the treatment of  symbolic  links.   Comâ€[m
       mand-line  arguments  following these are taken to be names of files or diâ€[m
       rectories to be examined, up to the first argument that begins with `-', or[m
       the  argument  `('  or  `!'.  That argument and any following arguments are[m
       taken to be the expression describing what is to be searched  for.   If  no[m
       paths are given, the current directory is used.  If no expression is given,[m
       the expression [1m-print[0m is used  (but  you  should  probably  consider  using[m
       [1m-print0[0m instead, anyway).[m
[m
       This  manual  page talks about `options' within the expression list.  These[m
       options control the behaviour of [1mfind[0m but are specified  immediately  after[m
       the last path name.  The five `real' options [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m, [1m-P[0m, [1m-D[0m and [1m-O[0m must apâ€[m
       pear before the first path name, if at all.  A double dash [1m--[0m  could  theoâ€[m
       retically  be  used to signal that any remaining arguments are not options,[m
       but this does not really work due to the way [1mfind[0m determines the end of the[m

[25;1H[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[26;1H       The [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m options control the treatment of  symbolic  links.   Comâ€[m
[27;1H       mand-line  arguments  following these are taken to be names of [7mfiles[27m or diâ€[m
[28;1H       rectories to be examined, up to the first argument that begins with `-', or[m
[29;1H       the  argument  `('  or  `!'.  That argument and any following arguments are[m
[30;1H       taken to be the expression describing what is to be searched  for.   If  no[m
[31;1H       paths are given, the current directory is used.  If no expression is given,[m
[32;1H       the expression [1m-print[0m is used  (but  you  should  probably  consider  using[m
[33;1H       [1m-print0[0m instead, anyway).[m
[34;1H[m
[35;1H       This  manual  page talks about `options' within the expression list.  These[m
[36;1H       options control the behaviour of [1mfind[0m but are specified  immediately  after[m
[37;1H       the last path name.  The five `real' options [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m, [1m-P[0m, [1m-D[0m and [1m-O[0m must apâ€[m
[38;1H       pear before the first path name, if at all.  A double dash [1m--[0m  could  theoâ€[m
[39;1H       retically  be  used to signal that any remaining arguments are not options,[m
[40;1H       but this does not really work due to the way [1mfind[0m determines the end of the[m
[41;1H       following path arguments: it does that by reading until an expression arguâ€[m
       ment comes (which also starts with a `-').  Now, if a path  argument  would[m
       start  with a `-', then [1mfind[0m would treat it as expression argument instead.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       Thus, to ensure that all start points are taken as such, and especially  to[m
       prevent  that  wildcard patterns expanded by the calling shell are not misâ€[m
       takenly treated as expression arguments, it is generally  safer  to  prefix[m
       wildcards  or  dubious  path names with either `./' or to use absolute path[m
       names starting with '/'.[m
[m
       -P     Never follow symbolic links.  This is the default  behaviour.   When[m
              [1mfind[0m  examines  or prints information about [7mfiles[27m, and the file is a[m
              symbolic link, the information used shall be taken from the  properâ€[m
              ties of the symbolic link itself.[m
[m
       -L     Follow  symbolic  links.   When  [1mfind[0m examines or prints information[m
              about [7mfiles[27m, the information used shall be taken from the properties[m
              of  the file to which the link points, not from the link itself (unâ€[m
              less it is a broken symbolic link or [1mfind[0m is unable to  examine  the[m
              file to which the link points).  Use of this option implies [1m-noleaf[0m.[m
              If you later use the [1m-P[0m option, [1m-noleaf[0m will still be in effect.  If[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              [1m-L[0m is in effect and [1mfind[0m discovers a symbolic link to a subdirectory[m
              during its search, the subdirectory pointed to by the symbolic  link[m
              will be searched.[m
[m
              When  the  [1m-L[0m  option  is in effect, the [1m-type[0m predicate will always[m
              match against the type of the file that a symbolic  link  points  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              rather  than  the  link itself (unless the symbolic link is broken).[m
              Actions that can cause symbolic links to become broken while [1mfind[0m is[m
              executing  (for  example  [1m-delete[0m) can give rise to confusing behavâ€[m
              iour.  Using [1m-L[0m causes the [1m-lname[0m and [1m-ilname[0m predicates  always  to[m
              return false.[m
[m
       -H     Do  not  follow  symbolic links, except while processing the command[m
              line arguments.  When [1mfind[0m  examines  or  prints  information  about[m
              [7mfiles[27m,  the  information  used shall be taken from the properties of[m
              the symbolic link itself.  The only exception to this  behaviour  is[m
              when  a  file  specified on the command line is a symbolic link, and[m
              the link can be resolved.  For that situation, the information  used[m
              is taken from whatever the link points to (that is, the link is folâ€[m
              lowed).  The information about the link itself is used as a fallback[m
              if  the file pointed to by the symbolic link cannot be examined.  If[m
              [1m-H[0m is in effect and one of the paths specified on the  command  line[m
              is  a  symbolic  link to a directory, the contents of that directory[m
              will be examined (though of course [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m would prevent this).[m
[m
       If more than one of [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m is specified, each overrides the  others;[m
       the  last  one appearing on the command line takes effect.  Since it is the[m
       default, the [1m-P[0m option should be considered to be in effect  unless  either[m
       [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m is specified.[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 51 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       GNU  [1mfind[0m  frequently stats [7mfiles[27m during the processing of the command line[m
       itself, before any searching has begun.   These  options  also  affect  how[m
       those  arguments  are processed.  Specifically, there are a number of tests[m
       that compare [7mfiles[27m listed on the command line against a file  we  are  curâ€[m
       rently  considering.   In each case, the file specified on the command line[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 56 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       will have been examined and some of its properties will  have  been  saved.[m
       If  the  named file is in fact a symbolic link, and the [1m-P[0m option is in efâ€[m
       fect (or if neither [1m-H[0m nor [1m-L[0m were specified), the information used for the[m
       comparison  will be taken from the properties of the symbolic link.  Otherâ€[m
       wise, it will be taken from the properties of the file the link points  to.[m
       If  [1mfind[0m  cannot  follow  the link (for example because it has insufficient[m
       privileges or the link points to a nonexistent file) the properties of  the[m
       link itself will be used.[m
[m
       When  the  [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m options are in effect, any symbolic links listed as the[m
       argument of [1m-newer[0m will be dereferenced, and the timestamp  will  be  taken[m
       from  the  file  to which the symbolic link points.  The same consideration[m
       applies to [1m-newerXY[0m, [1m-anewer[0m and [1m-cnewer[0m.[m
[m
       The [1m-follow[0m option has a similar effect to [1m-L[0m, though it  takes  effect  at[m
       the  point where it appears (that is, if [1m-L[0m is not used but [1m-follow[0m is, any[m
       symbolic links appearing after [1m-follow[0m on the command line will be dereferâ€[m
       enced, and those before it will not).[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 75 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       -D debugopts[m
              Print  diagnostic information; this can be helpful to diagnose probâ€[m
              lems with why [1mfind[0m is not doing what you want.  The  list  of  debug[m
              options  should  be comma separated.  Compatibility of the debug opâ€[m
              tions is not guaranteed between releases of findutils.  For  a  comâ€[m
              plete  list  of valid debug options, see the output of [1mfind[0m [1m-D[0m [1mhelp[0m.[m
              Valid debug options include[m
[m
              exec   Show diagnostic information relating to -exec, -execdir,  -ok[m
                     and -okdir[m

[m
              tree   Show the expression tree in its original and optimised form.[m
[m
              all    Enable all of the other debug options (but [1mhelp[0m).[m

[m
       -Olevel[m
              Enables query optimisation.  The  [1mfind[0m  program  reorders  tests  to[m
              speed  up  execution  while  preserving the overall effect; that is,[m
              predicates with side effects are  not  reordered  relative  to  each[m
              other.   The  optimisations performed at each optimisation level are[m
              as follows.[m
[m
              0      Equivalent to optimisation level 1.[m
[m
              1      This is the default optimisation level and corresponds to the[m
                     traditional  behaviour.   Expressions  are  reordered so that[m
                     tests based only on the names of [7mfiles[27m (for example [1m-name[0m and[m
                     [1m-regex[0m) are performed first.[m
[m
              2      Any [1m-type[0m or [1m-xtype[0m tests are performed after any tests based[m
                     only on the names of [7mfiles[27m, but before any tests that require[m
                     information from the inode.  On many modern versions of Unix,[m
                     file types are returned by [1mreaddir()[0m and so these  predicates[m
                     are faster to evaluate than predicates which need to stat the[m
                     file first.  If you use the [1m-fstype[0m [4mFOO[24m predicate and specify[m
                     a [7mfiles[27mystem type [4mFOO[24m which is not known (that is, present in[m
                     `/etc/mtab') at the  time  [1mfind[0m  starts,  that  predicate  is[m
                     equivalent to [1m-false[0m.[m
[m
              3      At  this  optimisation level, the full cost-based query optiâ€[m
                     miser is enabled.  The order of tests  is  modified  so  that[m
                     cheap  (i.e.  fast) tests are performed first and more expenâ€[m
                     sive ones are performed later,  if  necessary.   Within  each[m
                     cost  band, predicates are evaluated earlier or later accordâ€[m
                     ing to whether they are likely to succeed or  not.   For  [1m-o[0m,[m
                     predicates which are likely to succeed are evaluated earlier,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 134 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K                     and for [1m-a[0m, predicates which are likely to fail are evaluated[m
                     earlier.[m
[m
              The  cost-based  optimiser  has a fixed idea of how likely any given[m
              test is to succeed.  In some cases the probability takes account  of[m
              the  specific nature of the test (for example, [1m-type[0m [1mf[0m is assumed to[m
              be more likely to succeed than [1m-type[0m [1mc[0m).  The  cost-based  optimiser[m
              is  currently  being evaluated.  If it does not actually improve the[m
              performance of [1mfind[0m, it will be removed again.  Conversely,  optimiâ€[m
              sations  that  prove to be reliable, robust and effective may be enâ€[m
              abled at lower optimisation levels over time.  However, the  default[m
              behaviour  (i.e.  optimisation  level  1) will not be changed in the[m
              4.3.x release series.  The findutils test suite runs all  the  tests[m
              on  [1mfind[0m  at  each optimisation level and ensures that the result is[m
              the same.[m
[m
[1mEXPRESSION[0m[m
       The part of the command line after the list of starting points is  the  [4mexâ€[24m[m
       [4mpression[24m.   This  is  a kind of query specification describing how we match[m
       [7mfiles[27m and what we do with the [7mfiles[27m that were matched.   An  expression  is[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 154 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       composed of a sequence of things:[m
[m
       Tests  Tests  return  a  true  or false value, usually on the basis of some[m
              property of a file we are considering.  The [1m-empty[0m test for  example[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 158 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              is true only when the current file is empty.[m
[m
       Actions[m
              Actions  have  side effects (such as printing something on the stanâ€[m
              dard output) and return either  true  or  false,  usually  based  on[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 163 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              whether  or  not they are successful.  The [1m-print[0m action for example[m
              prints the name of the current file on the standard output.[m
[m
       Global options[m
              Global options affect the operation of tests and  actions  specified[m
              on any part of the command line.  Global options always return true.[m
              The [1m-depth[0m option for example makes [1mfind[0m traverse the file system in[m
              a depth-first order.[m
[m
       Positional options[m
              Positional  options  affect only tests or actions which follow them.[m
              Positional options always return true.  The  [1m-regextype[0m  option  for[m
              example is positional, specifying the regular expression dialect for[m
              regular expressions occurring later on the command line.[m
[m
       Operators[m
              Operators join together the other items within the expression.  They[m
              include  for example [1m-o[0m (meaning logical OR) and [1m-a[0m (meaning logical[m
              AND).  Where an operator is missing, [1m-a[0m is assumed.[m
[m
       The [1m-print[0m action is performed on all [7mfiles[27m for which the whole  expression[m
       is  true, unless it contains an action other than [1m-prune[0m or [1m-quit[0m.  Actions[m
       which inhibit the default [1m-print[0m are [1m-delete[0m, [1m-exec[0m, [1m-execdir[0m, [1m-ok[0m, [1m-okdir[0m,[m
       [1m-fls[0m, [1m-fprint[0m, [1m-fprintf[0m, [1m-ls[0m, [1m-print[0m and [1m-printf[0m.[m
[m
       The [1m-delete[0m action also acts like an option (since it implies [1m-depth[0m).[m
[m
   [1mPOSITIONAL[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       Positional  options  always  return true.  They affect only tests occurring[m
       later on the command line.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 193 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       -daystart[m
              Measure times (for [1m-amin[0m, [1m-atime[0m, [1m-cmin[0m, [1m-ctime[0m, [1m-mmin[0m, and  [1m-mtime[0m)[m
              from the beginning of today rather than from 24 hours ago.  This opâ€[m
              tion only affects tests which appear later on the command line.[m
[m
       -follow[m
              Deprecated; use the [1m-L[0m option instead.  Dereference symbolic  links.[m
              Implies  [1m-noleaf[0m.  The [1m-follow[0m option affects only those tests which[m
              appear after it on the command line.  Unless the [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m option has[m
              been  specified,  the position of the [1m-follow[0m option changes the beâ€[m
              haviour of the [1m-newer[0m predicate; any [7mfiles[27m listed as the argument of[m
              [1m-newer[0m  will  be  dereferenced if they are symbolic links.  The same[m
              consideration applies to [1m-newerXY[0m, [1m-anewer[0m and [1m-cnewer[0m.   Similarly,[m

       -regextype [4mtype[24m[m
              Changes the regular  expression  syntax  understood  by  [1m-regex[0m  and[m
              [1m-iregex[0m  tests  which occur later on the command line.  To see which[m

              info  documentation  (see [1mSEE[0m [1mALSO[0m) explains the meaning of and difâ€[m
              ferences between the various types of regular expression.[m

       -warn, -nowarn[m
              Turn warning messages on or off.  These warnings apply only  to  the[m
              command  line usage, not to any conditions that [1mfind[0m might encounter[m
              when it searches directories.  The default behaviour corresponds  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 223 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              [1m-warn[0m  if  standard  input is a tty, and to [1m-nowarn[0m otherwise.  If a[m

   [1mGLOBAL[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       Global  options  always  return  true.  Global options take effect even for[m
       tests which occur earlier on  the  command  line.   To  prevent  confusion,[m
       global options should specified on the command-line after the list of start[m
       points, just before the first test, positional option or  action.   If  you[m
       specify a global option in some other place, [1mfind[0m will issue a warning mesâ€[m
       sage explaining that this can be confusing.[m
[m
       The global options occur after the list of start points, and so are not the[m
       same kind of option as [1m-L[0m, for example.[m
[m
       -d     A  synonym for -depth, for compatibility with FreeBSD, NetBSD, MacOS[m
              X and OpenBSD.[m
[m
       -depth Process each directory's contents before the directory itself.   The[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 244 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
              also  applies  to  [7mfiles[27m or directories whose names are given on the[m
              command line.  This option takes effect at the time the command line[m
              is read, which means that you cannot search one part of the [7mfiles[27mysâ€[m
              tem with this option on and part of it with this option off (if  you[m
              need  to  do that, you will need to issue two [1mfind[0m commands instead,[m
              one with the option and one without it).[m
[m
              Furthermore, [1mfind[0m with the [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m option  will  ignore[m
              errors  of  the  [1m-delete[0m action in the case the file has disappeared[m
              since the parent directory was read: it will not output an error diâ€[m
              agnostic, and the return code of the [1m-delete[0m action will be true.[m
[m
       -maxdepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Descend  at  most [4mlevels[24m (a non-negative integer) levels of directoâ€[m
              ries below the starting-points.  Using [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m means only  apply[m
              the tests and actions to the starting-points themselves.[m
[m
       -mindepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Do not apply any tests or actions at levels less than [4mlevels[24m (a non-[m
              negative integer).  Using [1m-mindepth[0m [1m1[0m means process all [7mfiles[27m except[m
              the starting-points.[m
[m
       -mount Don't  descend  directories on other [7mfiles[27mystems.  An alternate name[m
              for [1m-xdev[0m, for compatibility with some other versions of [1mfind[0m.[m
[m
       -noignore_readdir_race[m
              Turns off the effect of [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m.[m
[m
       -noleaf[m
              Do not optimize by assuming that directories contain 2 fewer  subdiâ€[m
              rectories  than  their  hard link count.  This option is needed when[m
              searching [7mfiles[27mystems that do not  follow  the  Unix  directory-link[m
              convention, such as CD-ROM or MS-DOS [7mfiles[27mystems or AFS volume mount[m
              points.  Each directory on a normal Unix [7mfiles[27mystem has at  least  2[m
              hard links: its name and its `.' entry.  Additionally, its subdirecâ€[m
              tories (if any) each have a `..' entry  linked  to  that  directory.[m
              When  [1mfind[0m  is  examining  a directory, after it has statted 2 fewer[m
              subdirectories than the directory's link count, it  knows  that  the[m
              rest  of  the  entries  in the directory are non-directories (`leaf'[m
              [7mfiles[27m in the directory tree).  If only the [7mfiles[27m' names need  to  be[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 294 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              examined,  there  is  no need to stat them; this gives a significant[m
              increase in search speed.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 296 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       -version, --version[m
              Print the [1mfind[0m version number and exit.[m
[m
       -xdev  Don't descend directories on other [7mfiles[27mystems.[m

       -Olevel[m

                     miser is enabled.  The order of tests  is  modified  so  that[m

                     sive ones are performed later,  if  necessary.   Within  each[m
                     cost  band, predicates are evaluated earlier or later accordâ€[m
                     ing to whether they are likely to succeed or  not.   For  [1m-o[0m,[m
                     predicates which are likely to succeed are evaluated earlier,[m

       -Olevel[m
              Enables query optimisation.  The  [1mfind[0m  program  reorders  tests  to[m
              speed  up  execution  while  preserving the overall effect; that is,[m
              predicates with side effects are  not  reordered  relative  to  each[m
              other.   The  optimisations performed at each optimisation level are[m
              as follows.[m
[m
              0      Equivalent to optimisation level 1.[m
[m
              1      This is the default optimisation level and corresponds to the[m
                     traditional  behaviour.   Expressions  are  reordered so that[m
                     tests based only on the names of [7mfiles[27m (for example [1m-name[0m and[m
                     [1m-regex[0m) are performed first.[m
[m
              2      Any [1m-type[0m or [1m-xtype[0m tests are performed after any tests based[m
                     only on the names of [7mfiles[27m, but before any tests that require[m
                     information from the inode.  On many modern versions of Unix,[m
                     file types are returned by [1mreaddir()[0m and so these  predicates[m
                     are faster to evaluate than predicates which need to stat the[m
                     file first.  If you use the [1m-fstype[0m [4mFOO[24m predicate and specify[m
                     a [7mfiles[27mystem type [4mFOO[24m which is not known (that is, present in[m
                     `/etc/mtab') at the  time  [1mfind[0m  starts,  that  predicate  is[m
                     equivalent to [1m-false[0m.[m
[m
              3      At  this  optimisation level, the full cost-based query optiâ€[m
                     miser is enabled.  The order of tests  is  modified  so  that[m
                     cheap  (i.e.  fast) tests are performed first and more expenâ€[m
                     sive ones are performed later,  if  necessary.   Within  each[m
                     cost  band, predicates are evaluated earlier or later accordâ€[m
                     ing to whether they are likely to succeed or  not.   For  [1m-o[0m,[m
                     predicates which are likely to succeed are evaluated earlier,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 134 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K                     and for [1m-a[0m, predicates which are likely to fail are evaluated[m
                     earlier.[m
[m
              The  cost-based  optimiser  has a fixed idea of how likely any given[m
              test is to succeed.  In some cases the probability takes account  of[m
              the  specific nature of the test (for example, [1m-type[0m [1mf[0m is assumed to[m
              be more likely to succeed than [1m-type[0m [1mc[0m).  The  cost-based  optimiser[m
              is  currently  being evaluated.  If it does not actually improve the[m
              performance of [1mfind[0m, it will be removed again.  Conversely,  optimiâ€[m
              sations  that  prove to be reliable, robust and effective may be enâ€[m
              abled at lower optimisation levels over time.  However, the  default[m
              behaviour  (i.e.  optimisation  level  1) will not be changed in the[m
              4.3.x release series.  The findutils test suite runs all  the  tests[m
              on  [1mfind[0m  at  each optimisation level and ensures that the result is[m
              the same.[m
[m
[1mEXPRESSION[0m[m
       The part of the command line after the list of starting points is  the  [4mexâ€[24m[m
       [4mpression[24m.   This  is  a kind of query specification describing how we match[m
       [7mfiles[27m and what we do with the [7mfiles[27m that were matched.   An  expression  is[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 154 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       composed of a sequence of things:[m
[m
       Tests  Tests  return  a  true  or false value, usually on the basis of some[m
              property of a file we are considering.  The [1m-empty[0m test for  example[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 158 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              is true only when the current file is empty.[m
[m
       Actions[m
              Actions  have  side effects (such as printing something on the stanâ€[m
              dard output) and return either  true  or  false,  usually  based  on[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 163 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              whether  or  not they are successful.  The [1m-print[0m action for example[m
              prints the name of the current file on the standard output.[m
[m
       Global options[m
              Global options affect the operation of tests and  actions  specified[m
              on any part of the command line.  Global options always return true.[m
              The [1m-depth[0m option for example makes [1mfind[0m traverse the file system in[m
              a depth-first order.[m
[m
       Positional options[m
              Positional  options  affect only tests or actions which follow them.[m
              Positional options always return true.  The  [1m-regextype[0m  option  for[m
              example is positional, specifying the regular expression dialect for[m
              regular expressions occurring later on the command line.[m
[m
       Operators[m
              Operators join together the other items within the expression.  They[m
              include  for example [1m-o[0m (meaning logical OR) and [1m-a[0m (meaning logical[m
              AND).  Where an operator is missing, [1m-a[0m is assumed.[m
[m
       The [1m-print[0m action is performed on all [7mfiles[27m for which the whole  expression[m
       is  true, unless it contains an action other than [1m-prune[0m or [1m-quit[0m.  Actions[m
       which inhibit the default [1m-print[0m are [1m-delete[0m, [1m-exec[0m, [1m-execdir[0m, [1m-ok[0m, [1m-okdir[0m,[m
       [1m-fls[0m, [1m-fprint[0m, [1m-fprintf[0m, [1m-ls[0m, [1m-print[0m and [1m-printf[0m.[m
[m
       The [1m-delete[0m action also acts like an option (since it implies [1m-depth[0m).[m
[m
   [1mPOSITIONAL[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       Positional  options  always  return true.  They affect only tests occurring[m
       later on the command line.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 193 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       -daystart[m
              Measure times (for [1m-amin[0m, [1m-atime[0m, [1m-cmin[0m, [1m-ctime[0m, [1m-mmin[0m, and  [1m-mtime[0m)[m
              from the beginning of today rather than from 24 hours ago.  This opâ€[m
              tion only affects tests which appear later on the command line.[m
[m
       -follow[m
              Deprecated; use the [1m-L[0m option instead.  Dereference symbolic  links.[m
              Implies  [1m-noleaf[0m.  The [1m-follow[0m option affects only those tests which[m
              appear after it on the command line.  Unless the [1m-H[0m or [1m-L[0m option has[m
              been  specified,  the position of the [1m-follow[0m option changes the beâ€[m
              haviour of the [1m-newer[0m predicate; any [7mfiles[27m listed as the argument of[m
              [1m-newer[0m  will  be  dereferenced if they are symbolic links.  The same[m
              consideration applies to [1m-newerXY[0m, [1m-anewer[0m and [1m-cnewer[0m.   Similarly,[m
              the  [1m-type[0m  predicate will always match against the type of the file[m
              that a symbolic link points to rather than the link  itself.   Using[m
              [1m-follow[0m  causes  the  [1m-lname[0m [1mand[0m [1m-ilname[0m predicates always to return[m
              false.[m
[m
       -regextype [4mtype[24m[m
              Changes the regular  expression  syntax  understood  by  [1m-regex[0m  and[m
              [1m-iregex[0m  tests  which occur later on the command line.  To see which[m
              regular expression types are known, use [1m-regextype[0m [1mhelp[0m.   The  Texâ€[m
              info  documentation  (see [1mSEE[0m [1mALSO[0m) explains the meaning of and difâ€[m
              ferences between the various types of regular expression.[m
[m
       -warn, -nowarn[m
              Turn warning messages on or off.  These warnings apply only  to  the[m
              command  line usage, not to any conditions that [1mfind[0m might encounter[m
              when it searches directories.  The default behaviour corresponds  to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 223 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              [1m-warn[0m  if  standard  input is a tty, and to [1m-nowarn[0m otherwise.  If a[m
              warning message relating to command-line usage is produced, the exit[m
              status  of [1mfind[0m is not affected.  If the POSIXLY_CORRECT environment[m
              variable is set, and [1m-warn[0m is also used, it is not specified  which,[m
              if any, warnings will be active.[m
[m
   [1mGLOBAL[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       Global  options  always  return  true.  Global options take effect even for[m
       tests which occur earlier on  the  command  line.   To  prevent  confusion,[m
       global options should specified on the command-line after the list of start[m
       points, just before the first test, positional option or  action.   If  you[m
       specify a global option in some other place, [1mfind[0m will issue a warning mesâ€[m
       sage explaining that this can be confusing.[m
[m
       The global options occur after the list of start points, and so are not the[m
       same kind of option as [1m-L[0m, for example.[m
[m
       -d     A  synonym for -depth, for compatibility with FreeBSD, NetBSD, MacOS[m
              X and OpenBSD.[m
[m
       -depth Process each directory's contents before the directory itself.   The[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 244 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
              also  applies  to  [7mfiles[27m or directories whose names are given on the[m
              command line.  This option takes effect at the time the command line[m
              is read, which means that you cannot search one part of the [7mfiles[27mysâ€[m
              tem with this option on and part of it with this option off (if  you[m
              need  to  do that, you will need to issue two [1mfind[0m commands instead,[m
              one with the option and one without it).[m
[m
              Furthermore, [1mfind[0m with the [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m option  will  ignore[m
              errors  of  the  [1m-delete[0m action in the case the file has disappeared[m
              since the parent directory was read: it will not output an error diâ€[m
              agnostic, and the return code of the [1m-delete[0m action will be true.[m
[m
       -maxdepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Descend  at  most [4mlevels[24m (a non-negative integer) levels of directoâ€[m
              ries below the starting-points.  Using [1m-maxdepth[0m [1m0[0m means only  apply[m
              the tests and actions to the starting-points themselves.[m
[m
       -mindepth [4mlevels[24m[m
              Do not apply any tests or actions at levels less than [4mlevels[24m (a non-[m
              negative integer).  Using [1m-mindepth[0m [1m1[0m means process all [7mfiles[27m except[m
              the starting-points.[m
[m
       -mount Don't  descend  directories on other [7mfiles[27mystems.  An alternate name[m
              for [1m-xdev[0m, for compatibility with some other versions of [1mfind[0m.[m
[m
       -noignore_readdir_race[m
              Turns off the effect of [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m.[m
[m
       -noleaf[m
              Do not optimize by assuming that directories contain 2 fewer  subdiâ€[m
              rectories  than  their  hard link count.  This option is needed when[m
              searching [7mfiles[27mystems that do not  follow  the  Unix  directory-link[m
              convention, such as CD-ROM or MS-DOS [7mfiles[27mystems or AFS volume mount[m
              points.  Each directory on a normal Unix [7mfiles[27mystem has at  least  2[m
              hard links: its name and its `.' entry.  Additionally, its subdirecâ€[m
              tories (if any) each have a `..' entry  linked  to  that  directory.[m
              When  [1mfind[0m  is  examining  a directory, after it has statted 2 fewer[m
              subdirectories than the directory's link count, it  knows  that  the[m
              rest  of  the  entries  in the directory are non-directories (`leaf'[m
              [7mfiles[27m in the directory tree).  If only the [7mfiles[27m' names need  to  be[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 294 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              examined,  there  is  no need to stat them; this gives a significant[m
              increase in search speed.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 296 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       -version, --version[m
              Print the [1mfind[0m version number and exit.[m
[m
       -xdev  Don't descend directories on other [7mfiles[27mystems.[m
[m
   [1mTESTS[0m[m
       Some tests, for example [1m-newerXY[0m and [1m-samefile[0m,  allow  comparison  between[m
       the  file currently being examined and some reference file specified on the[m
       command line.  When these tests are used, the interpretation of the  referâ€[m
       ence file is determined by the options [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m and any previous [1m-folâ€[0m[m
       [1mlow[0m, but the reference file is only examined once, at the time the  command[m
       line is parsed.  If the reference file cannot be examined (for example, the[m
       [1mstat[0m(2) system call fails for it), an error message is issued, and [1mfind[0m exâ€[m
       its with a nonzero status.[m
[m
       A  numeric  argument [4mn[24m can be specified to tests (like [1m-amin[0m, [1m-mtime[0m, [1m-gid[0m,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 313 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       [1m-inum[0m, [1m-links[0m, [1m-size[0m, [1m-uid[0m and [1m-used[0m) as[m
[m
       [4m+n[24m     for greater than [4mn[24m,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 316 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       [4m-n[24m     for less than [4mn[24m,[m
[m
       [4mn[24m      for exactly [4mn[24m.[m
[m
       Supported tests:[m
[m
       -amin [4mn[24m[m
              File was last accessed less than, more than  or  exactly  [4mn[24m  minutes[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 325 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              ago.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 326 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 327 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K       -anewer [4mreference[24m[m
              Time of the last access of the current file is more recent than that[m
              of the last data modification of the [4mreference[24m file.   If  [4mreference[24m[m
              is  a symbolic link and the [1m-H[0m option or the [1m-L[0m option is in effect,[m
              then the time of the last data modification of the file it points to[m
              is always used.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 333 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K[m
       -atime [4mn[24m[m
              File  was  last  accessed less than, more than or exactly [4mn[24m*24 hours[m
              ago.  When find figures out how many 24-hour periods  ago  the  file[m
              was  last  accessed,  any  fractional  part  is ignored, so to match[m
              [1m-atime[0m [1m+1[0m, a file has to have been accessed at least [4mtwo[24m days ago.[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 340 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
              Matches [7mfiles[27m which are executable and directories which are searchâ€[m
              able (in a file name resolution sense) by the  current  user.   This[m
              takes  into account access control lists and other permissions arteâ€[m
              facts which the [1m-perm[0m test ignores.  This test makes use of the  [1macâ€[0m[m
              [1mcess[0m(2)  system  call,  and so can be fooled by NFS servers which do[m
              UID mapping (or root-squashing), since many  systems  implement  [1macâ€[0m[m
              [1mcess[0m(2)  in  the  client's  kernel and so cannot make use of the UID[m
              mapping information held on the server.  Because this test is  based[m
              only on the result of the [1maccess[0m(2) system call, there is no guaranâ€[m
              tee that a file for which this test succeeds can  actually  be  exeâ€[m
              cuted.[m
[m
       -false Always false.[m
[m
       -fstype [4mtype[24m[m
              File  is  on  a [7mfiles[27mystem of type [4mtype[24m.  The valid [7mfiles[27mystem types[m
              vary among  different  versions  of  Unix;  an  incomplete  list  of[m
              [7mfiles[27mystem  types  that  are accepted on some version of Unix or anâ€[m
              other is: ufs, 4.2, 4.3, nfs, tmp, mfs, S51K,  S52K.   You  can  use[m
              [1m-printf[0m with the %F directive to see the types of your [7mfiles[27mystems.[m
[m
       -gid [4mn[24m File's numeric group ID is less than, more than or exactly [4mn[24m.[m
[m
       -group [4mgname[24m[m
              File belongs to group [4mgname[24m (numeric group ID allowed).[m
[m
       -ilname [4mpattern[24m[m
              Like [1m-lname[0m, but the match is case insensitive.  If the [1m-L[0m option or[m
              the [1m-follow[0m option is in effect, this test returns false unless  the[m

       -iname [4mpattern[24m[m
              Like  [1m-name[0m,  but  the  match is case insensitive.  For example, the[m

       -iwholename [4mpattern[24m[m

       -links [4mn[24m[m

       -path [4mpattern[24m[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 481 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              File  [7mname[27m matches shell pattern [4mpattern[24m.  The metacharacters do not[m

              Find  compares the [1m-path[0m argument with the concatenation of a direcâ€[m
              tory [7mname[27m and the base [7mname[27m of the file it's examining.   Since  the[m

              a slash will match nothing (except perhaps a start  point  specified[m

       -perm [4mmode[24m[m

       -size [4mn[24m[cwbkMG][m
              File uses less than, more than or exactly [4mn[24m units of space, rounding[m
              up.  The following suffixes can be used:[m
[m
              `b'    for  512-byte  blocks  (this  is  the default if no suffix is[m
                     used)[m
[m
              `c'    for bytes[m
[m
              `w'    for two-byte words[m
[m
              `k'    for kibibytes (KiB, units of 1024 bytes)[m
[m
              `M'    for mebibytes (MiB, units of 1024 * 1024 = 1048576 bytes)[m
[m
              `G'    for gibibytes (GiB, units of 1024 * 1024 * 1024 =  1073741824[m
                     bytes)[m
[m
              The  size  is simply the st_size member of the struct stat populated[m
              by the lstat (or stat) system call, rounded up as shown  above.   In[m
              other  words,  it's  consistent  with  the result you get for [1mls[0m [1m-l[0m.[m
              Bear in mind that the `%k' and `%b'  format  specifiers  of  [1m-printf[0m[m
              handle  sparse  files  differently.   The  `b' suffix always denotes[m
              512-byte blocks and never 1024-byte blocks, which  is  different  to[m
              the behaviour of [1m-ls[0m.[m
[m
              The  +  and - prefixes signify greater than and less than, as usual;[m
              i.e., an exact size of [4mn[24m units does not match.  Bear  in  mind  that[m
              the size is rounded up to the next unit.  Therefore [1m-size[0m [1m-1M[0m is not[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 580 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              equivalent to [1m-size[0m [1m-1048576c[0m.  The former only matches empty files,[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 581 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              the latter matches files from 0 to 1,048,575 bytes.[m

   [1mACTIONS[0m[m
       -delete[m
              Delete files; true if removal succeeded.  If the removal failed,  an[m
              error  message is issued.  If [1m-delete[0m fails, [1mfind[0m's exit status will[m
              be nonzero (when it eventually exits).  Use of [1m-delete[0m automatically[m
              turns on the `[1m-depth[0m' option.[m
[m
              [1mWarnings[0m: Don't forget that the find command line is evaluated as an[m
              expression, so putting [1m-delete[0m first will make [1mfind[0m  try  to  delete[m
              everything  below the starting points you specified.  When testing a[m
              [1mfind[0m command line that you later intend to  use  with  [1m-delete[0m,  you[m
              should  explicitly specify [1m-depth[0m in order to avoid later surprises.[m
              Because [1m-delete[0m implies [1m-depth[0m, you cannot usefully use  [1m-prune[0m  and[m
              [1m-delete[0m together.[m
[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 656 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              Together  with the [1m-ignore_readdir_race[0m option, [1mfind[0m will ignore erâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 657 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              rors of the [1m-delete[0m action in the  case  the  file  has  disappeared[m
              since the parent directory was read: it will not output an error diâ€[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 659 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K...skipping...
              placed by the current file [7mname[27m being processed everywhere it occurs[m
              in the arguments to the command, not just in arguments where  it  is[m
              alone,  as  in  some  versions of [1mfind[0m.  Both of these constructions[m
              might need to be escaped (with a `\') or quoted to protect them from[m
              expansion  by  the  shell.  See the [1mEXAMPLES[0m section for examples of[m
              the use of the [1m-exec[0m option.  The specified command is run once  for[m
              each  matched  file.  The command is executed in the starting direcâ€[m
              tory.  There are unavoidable security problems  surrounding  use  of[m

       -exec [4mcommand[24m {} +[m
              This  variant  of the [1m-exec[0m action runs the specified command on the[m
              selected files, but the command line is built by appending each  seâ€[m
              lected  file [7mname[27m at the end; the total number of invocations of the[m
              command will be much less than the number  of  matched  files.   The[m
              command  line  is  built  in much the same way that [1mxargs[0m builds its[m
              command lines.  Only one instance of `{}' is allowed within the comâ€[m
              mand,  and it must appear at the end, immediately before the `+'; it[m
              needs to be escaped (with a `\') or quoted to protect it from interâ€[m
              pretation by the shell.  The command is executed in the starting diâ€[m
              rectory.  If any invocation with the `+'  form  returns  a  non-zero[m
              value  as exit status, then [1mfind[0m returns a non-zero exit status.  If[m
              [1mfind[0m encounters an error, this  can  sometimes  cause  an  immediate[m
              exit, so some pending commands may not be run at all.  For this reaâ€[m
              son [1m-exec[0m [4mmy-command[24m [1m...[0m [1m{}[0m [1m+[0m [1m-quit[0m may not result in [4mmy-command[24m acâ€[m
              tually being run.  This variant of [1m-exec[0m always returns true.[m
[m
       -execdir [4mcommand[24m ;[m
[m
       -execdir [4mcommand[24m {} +[m
              Like  [1m-exec[0m,  but the specified command is run from the subdirectory[m
              containing the matched file, which is not normally the directory  in[m
              which  you  started [1mfind[0m.  As with -exec, the {} should be quoted if[m
              find is being invoked from a shell.  This a much more secure  method[m
              for  invoking  commands, as it avoids race conditions during resoluâ€[m
              tion of the paths to the matched files.  As with the  [1m-exec[0m  action,[m
              the  `+'  form of [1m-execdir[0m will build a command line to process more[m
              than one matched file, but any given invocation of [4mcommand[24m will only[m
              list files that exist in the same subdirectory.  If you use this opâ€[m
              tion, you must ensure that your [1m$PATH[0m environment variable does  not[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 705 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K/[K              reference `.'; otherwise, an attacker can run any commands they like[m
              by leaving an appropriately-[7mname[27md file in a directory in  which  you[m
              will  run  [1m-execdir[0m.   The  same  applies to having entries in [1m$PATH[0m[m
              which are empty or which are not absolute directory [7mname[27ms.   If  any[m
              invocation  with  the `+' form returns a non-zero value as exit staâ€[m
              tus, then [1mfind[0m returns a non-zero exit status.  If  [1mfind[0m  encounters[m
              an  error, this can sometimes cause an immediate exit, so some pendâ€[m
              ing commands may not be run at all.  The result of  the  action  deâ€[m
              pends on whether the [1m+[0m or the [1m;[0m variant is being used; [1m-execdir[0m [4mcomâ€[24m[m
              [4mmand[24m [1m{}[0m [1m+[0m always returns true, while  [1m-execdir[0m [4mcommand[24m [1m{}[0m [1m;[0m  returns[m
              true only if [4mcommand[24m returns 0.[m
